# -
#  JTAG STRAP register setting
#  bit0: 0 	 - PBIST mode			Enable PBIST/DAT mode.When set, the device will enter DAT mode to be used by PBIST;
#  bit1: 0 	 - SCT mode			Self Control Timing;
#  bit2: 0 	 - LYA mode			Low Yield Analysis;
#  bit3: 1 	 - HRC mode			Enable HRC Mode.When set, the device will enter HRC (Half Reference Clock) mode;
#  bit4: 1 	 - PLL Reset			PLL Reset Counter.When set, the EBL reset counter (2^18) will be disabled.;
#  bit5: 1 	 - DCU Init Disable		DCU Init Disable.When set, the Ucode DCU init routine will be disabled.;
#  bit6: 1 	 - Load CR#0			Load CR#0 (Enables L1/L2 and MTRR 0x0806);
#  bit7: 0 	 - L2 Disable			L2 Disable.When set, the L2 will be disabled.;
#  bit8: 0 	 - Disable Bus Power Features	Disable Bus power reduction features;
#  bit9: 0 	 - Disable CPU Power Features	Disable CPU power reduction features;
#  bit10: 1 	 - Disable DFT pins strapping	Disable DFT pins to service for strapping;
#  bit11: 0 	 - Disable RCOMP execution	Disable RCOMP execution ;
#  bit12: 0 	 - Disable Quiet Cycle		Disable Quiet cycles;
#  bit13: 0 	 - BSCAN OEM/HVM mode		Select the boundary scan mode0 - OEM (Default Rcomp/Slew Rate)1 - HVM (Automatic Rcomp/Slew Rate);
#  bit14: 0 	 - ODT OFF			Control the On-Die TerminationWhen set, the ODT is OFF;
#  bit15: 1 	 - DFT clock enable		Enable DFT clocks for LCP and LSD chains;
#  bit16: 0 	 - FP-LCP Trigger		Force fusible/patchable LCP sequence;
#  bit17: 0 	 - PREQ Break Disable		Disable PREQ to break C3 mode;
#  bit18: 0 	 - HVM Short Cal		Force the EBL counter to count 100us (instead of 128ms) to enable Rcomp cycles in HVM;
#  bit19: 0 	 - On Die FRC			Enables on die FRC;
#  bit20: 0 	 - FRC Master			Sets On-Die FRC Master Core;
#  bit21: 0 	 - SBFT En			Sets SBFT Mode On;
#  bit22: 0 	 - Disable L2 Invalidation			Disable L2 Invalidation For SBFT Mode;
